  344                     <p class="blog-excerpt">Get stuck with a flat tire in Chiang Mai. Learn how to ac
      cess quick repairs through local ba yarng tire fixers who come to you.</p>

      ;">
  351             <div class="container" style="max-width: 960px;">
  352                 <!-- BLOG METADATA -->
  353                 <div class="blog-metadata reveal" style="padding: 0.75rem 0 0.75rem; margin-bottom: 1
      .5rem;">
  354                     <div class="blog-meta-item">
  355                         <span class="blog-meta-label">Category</span>
  356                         <span class="blog-meta-value"><a href="../" style="color: inherit; text-decor
      ation: none;">Home</a> / Daily Life / Transport</span>
  357                     </div>
  358                     <div class="blog-meta-divider"></div>

  360                         <span class="blog-meta-label">Read time</span>

  371
  372                     <!-- ARTICLE INTRO: Answer the main question in first 300 words -->
  373                     <div class="article-intro">
  374                         <h2>What Do You Do When Your Tire Goes Flat?</h2>
  375                         <p class="article-vibe">You don't have to push your motorbike to a mechanic.
      In Chiang Mai, flat tires are handled differently. Mobile tire fixers called ba yarng come to you and
       fix your tire on the spot within 10 to 15 minutes.</p>
  376                     </div>
  377
  378                     <p>
  379                         One of the great things about living in Chiang Mai is the ease of getting aro
      und on a motorbike. But what happens when your tire goes flat? Well, it's surprisingly easy. Instead
      of pushing your bike to a mechanic, you can simply give someone a call and they will come to you and
      fix your tire right where you are.
  380                     </p>
  381
  382                     <!-- IMAGE IN TOP RIGHT -->
  383                     <figure class="img-right-small" style="margin-top: -30px; margin-bottom: 1rem; wi
      dth: calc(100% - 400px); max-width: 300px;">
  384                         <img src="../images/chiang-mai-ambassador-chiangmaiambassador-Chiangmaiambass
      ador-flat-tire-tyre-3.webp" alt="Flat tire being repaired" width="300" height="225">
  385                     </figure>
  386
  387                     <!-- TL;DR: QUICK SUMMARY (placed early) -->
  388                     <div class="article-sidebar">
  389                         <h4>Quick Summary (TL;DR)</h4>
  390                         <ul>
  391                             <li>Flat tires don't require pushing to a mechanic in Chiang Mai</li>
  392                             <li>Ba yarng (ปะยาง) are mobile tire fixers that come to you</li>
  393                             <li>They arrive within 10 to 15 minutes of your call</li>
  394                             <li>You'll be back on your motorbike within about an hour</li>
  395                             <li>Look for phone numbers posted on power poles throughout Chiang Mai</l
      i>
  396                             <li>The service is reliable and affordable</li>
  397                             <li>They operate throughout the city</li>
  398                             <li>No need to visit a workshop for basic tire repairs</li>
  399                         </ul>
  400                     </div>
  401
  402                     <h3>The Ba Yarng Solution</h3>
  403                     <p>
  404                         It's called a ba yarng (ปะยาง), which translates to a motorbike tire fixer. T
      hey are all over the place in Chiang Mai. The local ba yarng will come and fix you up within about 10
       to 15 minutes. Most importantly, they'll have you back on your motorbike within about an hour. This
      is the local solution that most residents rely on.
  405                     </p>
  406
  407                     <!-- Three image layout -->
  408                     <figure class="img-float-right-small">
  409                         <img src="../images/chiang-mai-ambassador-chiangmaiambassador-Chiangmaiambass
      ador-flat-tire-tyre-8-1.webp" alt="Ba yarng tire repair equipment" width="400" height="300">
  410                     </figure>
  411
  412                     <p>
  413                         Finding a ba yarng is straightforward. Look at any power pole near you. They
      post their phone numbers on poles throughout Chiang Mai so you can call them when you need them. The
      system is simple, efficient, and has been working for years.
  414                     </p>
  415
  416                     <h3>How to Find a Ba Yarng</h3>
  417                     <p>
  418                         Power poles throughout Chiang Mai are covered with phone numbers for local ba
       yarng tire fixers. These aren't official businesses with fancy signage, they're local operators who
      have been repairing tires for residents for years. When you need a tire fixed, simply look for the ne
      arest power pole and call one of the numbers posted there.
  419                     </p>
  420
  421                     <!-- Additional images -->
  422                     <figure class="img-fullwidth-break">
  423                         <img src="../images/chiang-mai-ambassador-chiangmaiambassador-Chiangmaiambass
      ador-flat-tire-tyre-6.webp" alt="Ba yarng phone numbers on power poles" width="900" height="500">
  424                     </figure>
  425
  426                     <p>
  427                         These pics were taken all over Chiang Mai, showing just how common and access
      ible these services are throughout the city.
  428                     </p>
  429
  430                     <!-- Final image -->
  431                     <figure class="img-fullwidth-break">
  432                         <img src="../images/chiang-mai-ambassador-chiangmaiambassador-Chiangmaiambass
      ador-flat-tire-tyre-9.webp" alt="Power poles with ba yarng contact information" width="900" height="5
      00">
  433                     </figure>
  434
  435                     <h3>Why This System Works</h3>
  436                     <p>
  437                         The ba yarng system is perfect for Chiang Mai because it's decentralized and
      fast. Rather than waiting for a tow truck or pushing your bike across town, a local fixer comes to yo
      u. This approach keeps you mobile and gets you back on the road quickly.
  438                     </p>
  439
  440                     <!-- KEY TAKEAWAYS -->
  441                     <div class="key-takeaways">
  442                         <h3>Key Takeaways</h3>
  443                         <p>
  444                             When you get a flat tire in Chiang Mai, don't panic. Look for a ba yarng
      phone number on a nearby power pole and call them. They'll come to you within 15 minutes and have you
       back on the road within the hour. It's a simple, local solution that residents rely on every day.
  445                         </p>
  446                     </div>
  447
  448                 </div>

   # For each file, extract main content section
   function Get-BlogContent {
       param([string]$filePath)
       $content = Get-Content $filePath -Raw

       if ($content -match '<article[^>]*class="[^"]*entry-content[^"]*"[^>]*>(.*?)<\/article>') {
           return $matches[1]
       } elseif ($content -match '<div[^>]*class="[^"]*entry-content[^"]*"[^>]*>(.*?)<\/div>\s*<footer') {
           return $matches[1]
       } elseif ($content -match '<main[^>]*>(.*?)<\/main>') {
           return $matches[1]
       }
       } elseif ($content -match '<main[^>]*>(.*?)<\/main>') {
           return $matches[1]
       }
  each batch.

 PowerShell command


   # Extract content from WordPress HTML and convert to clean text
   function Extract-BlogContent {
       param([string]$filePath)

       $html = Get-Content $filePath -Raw

       # Extract title from page title
       $titleMatch = $html -match '<title>([^|<]+)'
       $title = if ($titleMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() } else { "Untitled" }

       # Extract first paragraph as excerpt
       if ($html -match '<p[^>]*>([^<]{50,200})<\/p>') {
           $excerpt = $matches[1].Trim() -replace '<[^>]+>', ''
           $excerpt = if ($excerpt.Length -gt 150) { $excerpt.Substring(0, 150) + "..." } else { $excerpt }
       } else {
           $excerpt = "Read more about this topic"
       }

       # Extract all paragraphs
       $paragraphs = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<p[^>]*>([^<]*(?:<[^/][^>]*>[^<]*)*)<\/p>') | ForEach-Object {
           $p = $_.Groups[1].Value -replace '<[^>]+>', ''
           $p = $p.Trim()
           if ($p.Length -gt 20) {
               $paragraphs += $p
           }
       }

       # Extract headings
       $h2s = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<h2[^>]*>([^<]+)<\/h2>') | ForEach-Object {
           $h2s += $_.Groups[1].Value.Trim()
       }
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<h2[^>]*>([^<]+)<\/h2>') | ForEach-Object {
           $h2s += $_.Groups[1].Value.Trim()
       }

               # Create blog filename

               # Move file to done folder first

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 PowerShell command


   # Complete content extractor function
   function Extract-AllContent {
       param([string]$filePath)

       $html = Get-Content $filePath -Raw

       # Extract title
       $titleMatch = $html -match '<title>([^|<]+)'
       $title = if ($titleMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() } else { "Untitled" }

       # Extract first paragraph as excerpt
       $excerptMatch = $html -match '<p[^>]*>([^<]{30,250})<\/p>'
       $excerpt = if ($excerptMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() -replace '<[^>]+>', '' } else { "Read this
   article" }

       # Extract ALL paragraphs in order
       $paragraphs = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<p[^>]*>([^<]+(?:<[^/][^>]*>[^<]*)*)<\/p>') | ForEach-Object {
           $p = $_.Groups[1].Value -replace '<[^>]+>', '' -replace '&nbsp;', ' ' -replace '&amp;', '&'
   -replace '&quot;', '"' -replace '&apos;', "'"
           $p = $p.Trim()
           if ($p.Length -gt 20) {
               $paragraphs += $p
           }
       }

       # Extract all headings with type
       $headings = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<h([1-6])[^>]*>([^<]+)<\/h[1-6]>') | ForEach-Object {
           $level = $_.Groups[1].Value
           $text = $_.Groups[2].Value.Trim()
           $headings += @{level = $level; text = $text}
       }

       # Extract all images
       $images = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, 'src="([^"]*\.webp)"[^>]*alt="([^"]*)"') | ForEach-Object {
           $src = $_.Groups[1].Value
           $alt = $_.Groups[2].Value
           $images += @{src = $src; alt = $alt}
       }

       return @{
           title = $title
           excerpt = $excerpt
           paragraphs = $paragraphs
           headings = $headings
           excerpt = $excerpt
           paragraphs = $paragraphs
           headings = $headings

   # Blog HTML builder with COMPLETE content
   function Build-CompleteBlog {
       param(
           [string]$fileName,
           [PSObject]$content,
           [string]$category,
           [string]$readTime
       )

       # Build TL;DR from actual content
       $tldrPoints = @()
       if ($content.paragraphs.Count -gt 0) {
           # Take key sentences from paragraphs
           $tldrPoints += $content.paragraphs[0].Substring(0, [Math]::Min(100,
   $content.paragraphs[0].Length))
           if ($content.paragraphs.Count -gt 1) {
               $tldrPoints += $content.paragraphs[1].Substring(0, [Math]::Min(100,
   $content.paragraphs[1].Length))
           }
           if ($content.paragraphs.Count -gt 2) {
               $tldrPoints += $content.paragraphs[2].Substring(0, [Math]::Min(100,
   $content.paragraphs[2].Length))
           }
       }

       $tldrHtml = "<div class='article-sidebar'><h4>Quick Summary (TL;DR)</h4><ul>"
       $tldrPoints | ForEach-Object {
           $tldrHtml += "<li>$_</li>"
       }
       $tldrHtml += "</ul></div>"

       # Build body content from all paragraphs and headings
       $bodyHtml = "<div class='article-intro'><h2>Overview</h2><p
   class='article-vibe'>$($content.excerpt)</p></div>"

       # Add all paragraphs
       $content.paragraphs | ForEach-Object {
           $bodyHtml += "<p>$_</p>"
       }

       # Add key takeaways
       $bodyHtml += "<div class='key-takeaways'><h3>Key Takeaways</h3>"
       $bodyHtml += "<p>$($content.paragraphs[0])</p>"
       $bodyHtml += "</div>"

       # Build complete HTML
       $html = @"
   <!DOCTYPE html>
   <html lang="en">
   <head>
       <meta charset="UTF-8">
       <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
       <meta name="description" content="$($content.excerpt)">
       <meta name="robots" content="index, follow">
       <title>$($content.title) | Chiang Mai Ambassador</title>
       <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/tokens.css">
       <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/base.css">
       <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/sections.css">
       <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/components.css">
       <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/blog.css">
       <link rel="preload" href="../fonts/outfit-600.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin>
       <link rel="preload" href="../fonts/outfit-800.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin>
       <link rel="preload" href="../fonts/plus-jakarta-400.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin>
       <link rel="preload" href="../fonts/plus-jakarta-500.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin>
       <style>

   0!important}.blog-hero{margin-top:80px}.img-right-small{float:right;width:30%;margin:0 0 1rem
   2rem;shape-margin:1rem}.article-sidebar{background:#f0d080;padding:2rem;border-left:4px solid
   var(--color-primary);border-radius:0;margin:2.5rem 0 3rem 0;border:1px solid #e5ddd0}.article-sidebar
   h4{font-size:1rem;color:#1a1a1a;margin:0 0 1.25rem
   0;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.05em}.article-sidebar
   ul{list-style:none;padding:0;margin:0}.article-sidebar li{color:#333;font-size:0.95rem;line-height:1.6;m
   argin-bottom:0.75rem}.blog-metadata{display:flex;align-items:center;gap:1.5rem;padding:2rem 0
   2.5rem;border-bottom:1px solid
   #e5ddd0;margin-bottom:2rem}.blog-meta-label{font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:0.1em;text-
   transform:uppercase;color:#999}.blog-meta-value{font-size:0.95rem;color:#333;font-weight:500}.blog-body
   h2{font-size:2rem;color:#1a1a1a;margin:2.5rem 0 1rem 0}.blog-body

   # COMPLETE EXTRACTION AND REBUILD SCRIPT - All functions + execution in one block

   # Function 1: Extract all content
   function Extract-AllContent {
       param([string]$filePath)

       $html = Get-Content $filePath -Raw

       $titleMatch = $html -match '<title>([^|<]+)'
       $title = if ($titleMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() } else { "Untitled" }

       $excerptMatch = $html -match '<p[^>]*>([^<]{30,250})<\/p>'
       $excerpt = if ($excerptMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() -replace '<[^>]+>', '' } else { "Read this
   article" }

       $paragraphs = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<p[^>]*>([^<]+(?:<[^/][^>]*>[^<]*)*)<\/p>') | ForEach-Object {
           $p = $_.Groups[1].Value -replace '<[^>]+>', '' -replace '&nbsp;', ' ' -replace '&amp;', '&'
   -replace '&quot;', '"'
           $p = $p.Trim()
           if ($p.Length -gt 20 -and $p.Length -lt 1000) {
               $paragraphs += $p
           }
       }

       return @{ title = $title; excerpt = $excerpt; paragraphs = $paragraphs }
   }

   # Function 2: Build complete blog HTML
   function Build-CompleteBlog {
       param([PSObject]$content, [string]$category, [string]$readTime)

       # Build body with ALL paragraphs
       $bodyHtml = "<div class='article-intro'><h2>Overview</h2><p
   class='article-vibe'>$($content.excerpt)</p></div>`n`n"
       $content.paragraphs | ForEach-Object {
           $bodyHtml += "<p>$_</p>`n"
       }

       # Build TL;DR from first paragraphs
       $tldrHtml = "<div class='article-sidebar'><h4>Quick Summary (TL;DR)</h4><ul>`n"
       $content.paragraphs | Select-Object -First 5 | ForEach-Object {
           $summary = if ($_.Length -gt 120) { $_.Substring(0, 120) + "..." } else { $_ }
           $tldrHtml += "<li>$summary</li>`n"
       }
       $tldrHtml += "</ul></div>`n"

       # Add key takeaways
       $bodyHtml += "<div class='key-takeaways'><h3>Key Takeaways</h3>`n"
       if ($content.paragraphs.Count -gt 0) {
           $bodyHtml += "<p>$($content.paragraphs[0])</p>`n"
       }
       $bodyHtml += "</div>"

       # Combine TL;DR and body
       $fullBody = $tldrHtml + "`n" + $bodyHtml

       # Build complete HTML document
       $html = @"
   <!DOCTYPE html><html lang="en"><head><meta charset="UTF-8"><meta name="viewport"
   content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0"><meta name="description"
   content="$($content.excerpt)"><meta name="robots" content="index, follow"><title>$($content.title) |
   Chiang Mai Ambassador</title><link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/tokens.css"><link rel="stylesheet"
   href="../css/base.css"><link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/sections.css"><link rel="stylesheet"
   href="../css/components.css"><link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/blog.css"><link rel="preload"
   href="../fonts/outfit-600.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin><link rel="preload"
   href="../fonts/outfit-800.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin><link rel="preload"
   href="../fonts/plus-jakarta-400.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin><link rel="preload"
   href="../fonts/plus-jakarta-500.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2"
   crossorigin><style>.blog-content{background-color:white!important;padding:5rem
   0!important}.blog-hero{margin-top:80px}.article-sidebar{background:#f0d080;padding:2rem;border-left:4px
   solid var(--color-primary);margin:2.5rem 0 3rem 0;border:1px solid #e5ddd0}.article-sidebar
   h4{font-size:1rem;color:#1a1a1a;margin:0 0 1.25rem
   0;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase}.article-sidebar
   ul{list-style:none;padding:0;margin:0}.article-sidebar li{color:#333;font-size:0.95rem;line-height:1.6;m
   argin-bottom:0.75rem}.blog-metadata{display:flex;gap:1.5rem;padding:2rem 0 2.5rem;border-bottom:1px
   solid #e5ddd0;margin-bottom:2rem}.blog-meta-label{font-size:0.75rem;font-weight:600;text-transform:upper
   case;color:#999}.blog-meta-value{font-size:0.95rem;color:#333}.blog-body
   h2{font-size:2rem;color:#1a1a1a;margin:2.5rem 0 1rem 0}.blog-body
   h3{font-size:1.25rem;color:#1a1a1a;margin:1.75rem 0 0.75rem 0}.blog-body p{font-size:1rem;color:#333;mar
   gin-bottom:1.5rem;line-height:1.8}.key-takeaways{background:#f0d080;padding:2rem;margin:3rem
   0;border:1px solid #e5ddd0}.key-takeaways h3{margin-top:0}.blog-related{padding:4rem

   # Image matching and blog rebuilding with images

   function Match-ImagesToProject {
       param([string]$sourceImagePath)

       # Extract the image identifier from source path
       # From: ../images/Chiang-Mai-Ambassador-37.jpg_54671c.webp
       # Extract: Chiang-Mai-Ambassador-37

       $filename = Split-Path $sourceImagePath -Leaf
       $filename = $filename -replace '_54671c\.(webp|jpg|png)', '' -replace '\.jpg$', '' -replace
   '\.png$', ''

       # Find matching image in project folder
       $projectFolder = "C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images"
       $matches = Get-ChildItem $projectFolder -Filter "*$filename*" -Name 2>$null

       if ($matches.Count -gt 0) {
           # Return the first match (there should only be one)
           return $matches[0] -replace '^', '../images/'
       }

       return $null
   }

       return $null
   }

   # Better image matching function
   function Find-ProjectImage {
       param([string]$sourceImagePath)

       # Extract base filename without extensions and cache busting
       $filename = Split-Path $sourceImagePath -Leaf

       # Remove common suffixes: _54671c, .webp, .jpg, .png
       $base = $filename -replace '_54671c\.(webp|jpg|png)$', '' -replace '\.(webp|jpg|png)$', ''

       # Search in project folder
       $projectFolder = "C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images"
       $found = @(Get-ChildItem $projectFolder -Filter "*$base*" -Name -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue)

       if ($found.Count -gt 0) {
           return "../images/$($found[0])"
       }
       return $null
   }

   # Test with cleaner logic

   # COMPLETE IMAGE INTEGRATION AND BLOG REBUILD

   function Find-ProjectImage {
       param([string]$sourceImagePath)
       $filename = Split-Path $sourceImagePath -Leaf
       $base = $filename -replace '_54671c\.(webp|jpg|png)$', '' -replace '\.(webp|jpg|png)$', ''
       $projectFolder = "C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images"
       $found = @(Get-ChildItem $projectFolder -Filter "*$base*" -Name -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue)
       if ($found.Count -gt 0) {
           return "../images/$($found[0])"
       }
       return $null
   }

   function Extract-ContentWithImages {
       param([string]$filePath)

       $html = Get-Content $filePath -Raw

       # Extract title and excerpt
       $titleMatch = $html -match '<title>([^|<]+)'
       $title = if ($titleMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() } else { "Untitled" }

       $excerptMatch = $html -match '<p[^>]*>([^<]{30,250})<\/p>'
       $excerpt = if ($excerptMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() -replace '<[^>]+>', '' } else { "Read this
   article" }

       # Extract all images with their alt text
       $images = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<img[^>]+src="([^"]*)"[^>]*alt="([^"]*)"') | ForEach-Object {
           $src = $_.Groups[1].Value
           $alt = $_.Groups[2].Value.Trim()
           $projectImage = Find-ProjectImage $src
           if ($projectImage) {
               $images += @{path = $projectImage; alt = $alt}
           }
       }

       # Extract all paragraphs
       $paragraphs = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<p[^>]*>([^<]+(?:<[^/][^>]*>[^<]*)*)<\/p>') | ForEach-Object {
           $p = $_.Groups[1].Value -replace '<[^>]+>', '' -replace '&nbsp;', ' ' -replace '&amp;', '&'
   -replace '&quot;', '"'
           $p = $p.Trim()
           if ($p.Length -gt 20 -and $p.Length -lt 1000) {
               $paragraphs += $p
           }
       }

       return @{
           title = $title
           excerpt = $excerpt
           paragraphs = $paragraphs
           images = $images
       }
   }

   function Build-BlogWithImages {
       param([PSObject]$content, [string]$category, [string]$readTime)

       # Build body with paragraphs and images interspersed
       $bodyHtml = "<div class='article-intro'><h2>Overview</h2><p
   class='article-vibe'>$($content.excerpt)</p></div>`n`n"

       # Add paragraphs with images every 3-4 paragraphs
       $paraCount = 0
       $imgIndex = 0

       $content.paragraphs | ForEach-Object {
           $bodyHtml += "<p>$_</p>`n"
           $paraCount++

           # Insert image every 3-4 paragraphs if available
           if ($paraCount -ge 3 -and $imgIndex -lt $content.images.Count) {
               $img = $content.images[$imgIndex]
               $bodyHtml += "<figure class='img-right-small'><img src='$($img.path)' alt='$($img.alt)'
   width='400' height='300'></figure>`n"
               $imgIndex++
               $paraCount = 0
           }
       }

       # Add remaining images after content
       while ($imgIndex -lt $content.images.Count) {
           $img = $content.images[$imgIndex]
           $bodyHtml += "<figure class='img-fullwidth-break'><img src='$($img.path)' alt='$($img.alt)'
   width='900' height='600'></figure>`n"
           $imgIndex++
       }

       # Build TL;DR
       $tldrHtml = "<div class='article-sidebar'><h4>Quick Summary (TL;DR)</h4><ul>`n"
       $content.paragraphs | Select-Object -First 5 | ForEach-Object {
           $summary = if ($_.Length -gt 120) { $_.Substring(0, 120) + "..." } else { $_ }
           $tldrHtml += "<li>$summary</li>`n"
       }
       $tldrHtml += "</ul></div>`n"

       # Add key takeaways
       $bodyHtml += "<div class='key-takeaways'><h3>Key Takeaways</h3>`n"
       if ($content.paragraphs.Count -gt 0) {
           $bodyHtml += "<p>$($content.paragraphs[0])</p>`n"
       }
       $bodyHtml += "</div>"

       $fullBody = $tldrHtml + "`n" + $bodyHtml

       # Build HTML
       $html = @"

   content="$($content.excerpt)"><meta name="robots" content="index, follow"><title>$($content.title) |
   Chiang Mai Ambassador</title><link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/tokens.css"><link rel="stylesheet"
   href="../css/base.css"><link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/sections.css"><link rel="stylesheet"
   href="../css/components.css"><link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/blog.css"><link rel="preload"
   href="../fonts/outfit-600.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin><link rel="preload"
   href="../fonts/outfit-800.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin><link rel="preload"
   href="../fonts/plus-jakarta-400.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin><link rel="preload"
   href="../fonts/plus-jakarta-500.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2"
   crossorigin><style>.blog-content{background-color:white!important;padding:5rem

   # FIXED: Extract content with proper image detection

   function Extract-ContentWithImages-Fixed {
       param([string]$filePath)

       $html = Get-Content $filePath -Raw

       # Title and excerpt
       $titleMatch = $html -match '<title>([^|<]+)'
       $title = if ($titleMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() } else { "Untitled" }

       $excerptMatch = $html -match '<p[^>]*>([^<]{30,250})<\/p>'
       $excerpt = if ($excerptMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() -replace '<[^>]+>', '' } else { "Read this
   article" }

       # Extract images - just get src
       $images = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<img[^>]*src="([^"]*)"[^>]*(?:alt="([^"]*)"|[^>]*)') | ForEach-Object {
           $src = $_.Groups[1].Value
           $alt = $_.Groups[2].Value

           # Filter out header/logo images
           if ($src -notmatch 'cropped|logo|header' -and $src -match '\.webp') {
               $projectImage = Find-ProjectImage $src
               if ($projectImage) {
                   $images += @{path = $projectImage; alt = if ($alt) { $alt } else { "Image" }}
               }
           }
       }

       # Extract paragraphs
       $paragraphs = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<p[^>]*>([^<]+(?:<[^/][^>]*>[^<]*)*)<\/p>') | ForEach-Object {
           $p = $_.Groups[1].Value -replace '<[^>]+>', '' -replace '&nbsp;', ' ' -replace '&amp;', '&'
   -replace '&quot;', '"'
           $p = $p.Trim()
           if ($p.Length -gt 20 -and $p.Length -lt 1000) {
               $paragraphs += $p
           }
       }

       return @{
           title = $title
           excerpt = $excerpt
           paragraphs = $paragraphs
           images = $images
       }
   }
           images = $images
       }
   }

   # COMPLETE ONE-SHOT: Image matching + content extraction + blog rebuild with images

   # Helper function: match source images to project images
   function Find-ProjectImage {
       param([string]$sourceImagePath)
       $filename = Split-Path $sourceImagePath -Leaf
       $base = $filename -replace '_54671c\.(webp|jpg|png)$', '' -replace '\.(webp|jpg|png)$', ''
       $projectFolder = "C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images"
       $found = @(Get-ChildItem $projectFolder -Filter "*$base*" -Name -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue)
       if ($found.Count -gt 0) { return "../images/$($found[0])" }
       return $null
   }

   # Extract all content + images
   function Extract-Full {
       param([string]$file)
       $html = Get-Content $file -Raw
       $titleMatch = $html -match '<title>([^|<]+)'
       $title = if ($titleMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() } else { "Untitled" }
       $excerptMatch = $html -match '<p[^>]*>([^<]{30,250})<\/p>'
       $excerpt = if ($excerptMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() -replace '<[^>]+>', '' } else { "Read this
   article" }

       $images = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<img[^>]*src="([^"]*)"') | ForEach-Object {
           $src = $_.Groups[1].Value
           if ($src -notmatch 'cropped|logo|header' -and $src -match '\.webp') {
               $proj = Find-ProjectImage $src
               if ($proj) { $images += $proj }
           }
       }

       $paragraphs = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<p[^>]*>([^<]+(?:<[^/][^>]*>[^<]*)*)<\/p>') | ForEach-Object {
           $p = $_.Groups[1].Value -replace '<[^>]+>', '' -replace '&nbsp;', ' ' -replace '&amp;', '&'
           $p = $p.Trim()
           if ($p.Length -gt 20 -and $p.Length -lt 1000) { $paragraphs += $p }
       }

       return @{title=$title; excerpt=$excerpt; paragraphs=$paragraphs; images=$images}
   }

   # Build blog HTML with images
   function Build-BlogHTML {
       param($content, $cat, $time)

       $body = "<div class='article-intro'><h2>Overview</h2><p
   class='article-vibe'>$($content.excerpt)</p></div>`n"
       $paraCount = 0
       $imgIdx = 0

       $content.paragraphs | ForEach-Object {
           $body += "<p>$_</p>`n"
           $paraCount++
           if ($paraCount -ge 3 -and $imgIdx -lt $content.images.Count) {
               $body += "<figure class='img-right-small'><img src='$($content.images[$imgIdx])' alt='Image'
    width='400' height='300'></figure>`n"
               $imgIdx++
               $paraCount = 0
           }
       }

       while ($imgIdx -lt $content.images.Count) {
           $body += "<figure class='img-fullwidth-break'><img src='$($content.images[$imgIdx])' alt='Image'
    width='900' height='600'></figure>`n"
           $imgIdx++
       }

       $tldr = "<div class='article-sidebar'><h4>Quick Summary</h4><ul>`n"
       $content.paragraphs | Select-Object -First 5 | ForEach-Object {
           $s = if ($_.Length -gt 120) { $_.Substring(0,120)+"..." } else { $_ }
           $tldr += "<li>$s</li>`n"
       }
       $tldr += "</ul></div>`n"

       $body += "<div class='key-takeaways'><h3>Key
   Takeaways</h3>`n<p>$($content.paragraphs[0])</p>`n</div>"
       $fullBody = $tldr + "`n" + $body

   href="../fonts/plus-jakarta-400.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin><link rel="preload"
   href="../fonts/plus-jakarta-500.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2"
   crossorigin><style>.blog-content{background-color:white!important;padding:5rem

   2rem}.img-fullwidth-break{width:100%;margin:3rem
   0}.article-sidebar{background:#f0d080;padding:2rem;border-left:4px solid

   # Recreate the batch version with complete content + images
   function Find-ProjectImage {
       param([string]$sourceImagePath)
       $filename = Split-Path $sourceImagePath -Leaf
       $base = $filename -replace '_54671c\.(webp|jpg|png)$', '' -replace '\.(webp|jpg|png)$', ''
       $projectFolder = "C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images"
       $found = @(Get-ChildItem $projectFolder -Filter "*$base*" -Name -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue)
       if ($found.Count -gt 0) { return "../images/$($found[0])" }
       return $null
   }

   function Extract-Full {
       param([string]$file)
       $html = Get-Content $file -Raw
       $titleMatch = $html -match '<title>([^|<]+)'
       $title = if ($titleMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() } else { "Untitled" }
       $excerptMatch = $html -match '<p[^>]*>([^<]{30,250})<\/p>'
       $excerpt = if ($excerptMatch) { $matches[1].Trim() -replace '<[^>]+>', '' } else { "Read this
   article" }

       $images = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<img[^>]*src="([^"]*)"') | ForEach-Object {
           $src = $_.Groups[1].Value
           if ($src -notmatch 'cropped|logo|header' -and $src -match '\.webp') {
               $proj = Find-ProjectImage $src
               if ($proj) { $images += $proj }
           }
       }

       $paragraphs = @()
       [regex]::Matches($html, '<p[^>]*>([^<]+(?:<[^/][^>]*>[^<]*)*)<\/p>') | ForEach-Object {
           $p = $_.Groups[1].Value -replace '<[^>]+>', '' -replace '&nbsp;', ' ' -replace '&amp;', '&'
           $p = $p.Trim()
           if ($p.Length -gt 20 -and $p.Length -lt 1000) { $paragraphs += $p }
       }

       return @{title=$title; excerpt=$excerpt; paragraphs=$paragraphs; images=$images}
   }

   function Build-BlogHTML {
       param($content, $cat, $time)

       $body = "<div class='article-intro'><h2>Overview</h2><p
   class='article-vibe'>$($content.excerpt)</p></div>`n"
       $paraCount = 0
       $imgIdx = 0

       $content.paragraphs | ForEach-Object {
           $body += "<p>$_</p>`n"
           $paraCount++
           if ($paraCount -ge 3 -and $imgIdx -lt $content.images.Count) {
               $body += "<figure class='img-right-small'><img src='$($content.images[$imgIdx])' alt='Image'
    width='400' height='300'></figure>`n"
               $imgIdx++
               $paraCount = 0
           }
       }

       while ($imgIdx -lt $content.images.Count) {
           $body += "<figure class='img-fullwidth-break'><img src='$($content.images[$imgIdx])' alt='Image'
    width='900' height='600'></figure>`n"
           $imgIdx++
       }

       $tldr = "<div class='article-sidebar'><h4>Quick Summary</h4><ul>`n"
       $content.paragraphs | Select-Object -First 5 | ForEach-Object {
           $s = if ($_.Length -gt 120) { $_.Substring(0,120)+"..." } else { $_ }
           $tldr += "<li>$s</li>`n"
       }
       $tldr += "</ul></div>`n"

       $body += "<div class='key-takeaways'><h3>Key
   Takeaways</h3>`n<p>$($content.paragraphs[0])</p>`n</div>"
       $fullBody = $tldr + "`n" + $body

       $html = @"

 Bash command

   python3 << 'SCRIPT'
   import re
   import shutil
   from pathlib import Path
   from html.parser import HTMLParser

   SOURCE_DIR = Path(r'C:\New folder\BLOGS\done')
   TEMPLATE_PATH = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs\template.html')
   OUTPUT_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs')
   IMAGES_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images')

   # Read template once
   with open(TEMPLATE_PATH, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
       template = f.read()

   def extract_main_content(html_content):
       """Extract main article content from HTML"""
       # Remove scripts and styles
       html = re.sub(r'<script[^>]*>.*?</script>', '', html_content, flags=re.DOTALL)
       html = re.sub(r'<style[^>]*>.*?</style>', '', html_content, flags=re.DOTALL)

       # Find main content area
       main_match = re.search(r'<main[^>]*>(.*?)</main>', html, re.DOTALL)
       if not main_match:
           main_match = re.search(r'<article[^>]*>(.*?)</article>', html, re.DOTALL)
       if not main_match:
           body_match = re.search(r'<body[^>]*>(.*?)<footer', html, re.DOTALL)
           main_match = body_match if body_match else None

       if main_match:
           content = main_match.group(1)
       else:
           content = html

       # Remove nav and header
       content = re.sub(r'<nav[^>]*>.*?</nav>', '', content, flags=re.DOTALL)
       content = re.sub(r'<header[^>]*>.*?</header>', '', content, flags=re.DOTALL)

       # Extract text
       text = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '\n', content)
       text = re.sub(r'\n\s*\n+', '\n', text)

       lines = [l.strip() for l in text.split('\n') if len(l.strip()) > 15]
       return '\n\n'.join(lines[:100])

   def find_image_files(html_content):
       """Extract image filenames from HTML"""
       matches = re.findall(r'src=["\']([^"\']+\.webp["\'])', html_content)
       filenames = [m.split('/')[-1].replace('"', '') for m in matches]
       return filenames

   def match_image_to_project(source_filename):
       """Match source image to project folder"""
       # Strip cache busting suffix
       base = re.sub(r'_[a-f0-9]{6}\.webp$', '', source_filename)

       # Skip header/logo images
       if any(x in base.lower() for x in ['cropped', 'logo', 'header']):
           return None

       # Search for matching file
       for img_file in IMAGES_DIR.glob(f"*{base}*"):
           if img_file.suffix == '.webp':
               return img_file.name

       return None

   def build_blog_content(title, paragraphs, images_to_insert):
       """Build blog content with proper formatting"""
       content = f"""<div class="article-intro">
       <h2>{title}</h2>
       <p class="article-vibe">{paragraphs[0] if paragraphs else 'Blog content'}</p>
   </div>

   <p>{paragraphs[1] if len(paragraphs) > 1 else ''}</p>
   """

       # Insert images at logical intervals
       para_index = 2
       image_index = 0

       while para_index < len(paragraphs):
           # Add paragraph
           content += f"<p>{paragraphs[para_index]}</p>\n\n"

           # Insert image every 3-4 paragraphs
           if image_index < len(images_to_insert) and para_index % 3 == 0:
               img_file = images_to_insert[image_index]
               content += f"""<figure class="img-right-small">
       <img src="../images/{img_file}" alt="Article image" width="400" height="300">
   </figure>

   """
               image_index += 1

           para_index += 1

       return content

   def process_file(source_file):
       """Process a single source file"""
       print(f"Processing {source_file.name}...", end=' ')

       with open(source_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
           source_html = f.read()

       # Extract title and content
       title_match = re.search(r'<title>([^<]+)</title>', source_html)
       title = title_match.group(1).split('|')[0].strip() if title_match else "Blog Post"

       content_text = extract_main_content(source_html)
       paragraphs = [p.strip() for p in content_text.split('\n\n') if p.strip()]

       # Find images
       image_filenames = find_image_files(source_html)
       matched_images = [m for m in [match_image_to_project(img) for img in image_filenames] if m]

       # Build new blog
       blog_content = build_blog_content(title, paragraphs[:15], matched_images[:4])

       # Replace content in template
       new_blog = template
       new_blog = new_blog.replace('Your Blog Post Title <span class="gold-gradient-text">Goes
   Here</span>', f'{title}')

       # Find and replace the blog-body content
       body_pattern = r'(<div class="blog-body">)(.*?)(</div>\s*</div>\s*</article>)'
       new_blog = re.sub(body_pattern, f'\\1\n{blog_content}\n\\3', new_blog, flags=re.DOTALL)

       # Save to output
       output_file = OUTPUT_DIR / source_file.name
       new_blog = re.sub(body_pattern, f'\\1\n{blog_content}\n\\3', new_blog, flags=re.DOTALL)

       # Save to output
       output_file = OUTPUT_DIR / source_file.name

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 Bash command

   python3 << 'EOF'
   import re
   from pathlib import Path

   # Paths
   SOURCE_FILE = Path(r'C:\New folder\BLOGS\done\about.html')
   TEMPLATE_FILE = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs\template.html')
   OUTPUT_FILE = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs\about.html')
   IMAGES_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images')

   # Read source
   source_content = SOURCE_FILE.read_text(encoding='utf-8')

   # Extract title
   title_match = re.search(r'<title>([^<]+)</title>', source_content)
   title = title_match.group(1).split('|')[0].strip() if title_match else "Blog Post"

   # Extract clean body paragraphs
   body = re.sub(r'<script[^>]*>.*?</script>', '', source_content, flags=re.DOTALL)
   body = re.sub(r'<style[^>]*>.*?</style>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
   body = re.sub(r'<nav[^>]*>.*?</nav>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
   body = re.sub(r'<footer[^>]*>.*?</footer>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)

   # Get text between body tags
   body_match = re.search(r'<body[^>]*>(.*?)(?:<footer|</body>)', body, re.DOTALL)
   if body_match:
       body = body_match.group(1)

   # Convert to paragraphs
   text = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '\n', body)
   text = re.sub(r'\n\s*\n+', '\n', text)
   paragraphs = [p.strip() for p in text.split('\n') if len(p.strip()) > 20]

   # Remove duplicates and navigation items
   clean_paragraphs = []
   seen = set()
   skip_words = ['facebook', 'menu', 'search', 'cookie', 'privacy', 'necessary', 'advertisement']
   for p in paragraphs:
       if p not in seen and not any(skip in p.lower() for skip in skip_words):
           clean_paragraphs.append(p)
           seen.add(p)

   # Get images
   image_matches = re.findall(r'src=["\']([^"\']+\.webp["\'])', source_content)
   image_files = [m.split('/')[-1] for m in image_matches]

   # Match images to project folder
   def match_image(img_filename):
       base = re.sub(r'_[a-f0-9]{6}\.webp$', '', img_filename)
       if any(x in base.lower() for x in ['cropped', 'logo', 'header']):
           return None
       for f in IMAGES_DIR.glob(f"*{base}*"):
           if f.suffix == '.webp':
               return f.name
       return None

   matched_images = [m for m in [match_image(img) for img in image_files] if m]
   print(f"Title: {title}")
   print(f"Paragraphs: {len(clean_paragraphs)}")
   print(f"Images matched: {len(matched_images)}")
   print(f"Images: {matched_images[:3]}")

   # Read template
   template = TEMPLATE_FILE.read_text(encoding='utf-8')

   # Update title in template
   blog_html = template.replace(
       'Your Blog Post Title <span class="gold-gradient-text">Goes Here</span>',
       title
   )

   # Build body content with images placed strategically
   body_content = f'<div class="article-intro">\n'
   body_content += f'    <h2>{title}</h2>\n'
   body_content += f'    <p class="article-vibe">{clean_paragraphs[0] if clean_paragraphs else "Blog
   content"}</p>\n'
   body_content += f'</div>\n\n'

   # Add paragraphs with images placed every 4-5 paragraphs
   para_idx = 1
   img_idx = 0
   while para_idx < len(clean_paragraphs) and para_idx < 20:
       body_content += f'<p>{clean_paragraphs[para_idx]}</p>\n\n'

   img_idx = 0
   while para_idx < len(clean_paragraphs) and para_idx < 20:
       body_content += f'<p>{clean_paragraphs[para_idx]}</p>\n\n'

 Bash command

   python3 << 'SCRIPT'
   import re
   from pathlib import Path
   from html.parser import HTMLParser

   SOURCE_DIR = Path(r'C:\New folder\BLOGS\done')
   TEMPLATE_FILE = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs\template.html')
   OUTPUT_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs')
   IMAGES_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images')

   # Load all project images
   project_images = {f.name for f in IMAGES_DIR.glob('*.webp')}

   def find_image_in_project(source_filename):
       """Find matching image in project folder"""
       # Remove cache suffix
       base = re.sub(r'_[a-f0-9]{6}\.webp$', '', source_filename)

       # Skip logos/headers
       if any(x in base.lower() for x in ['cropped', 'logo', 'header']):
           return None

       # Find exact or close match
       for proj_img in project_images:
           if base.lower() in proj_img.lower() or proj_img.lower().startswith(base.lower()[:20]):
               return proj_img

       return None

   def extract_images_with_positions(html_content):
       """Extract images and their positions in the content"""
       # Find all <p> tags first
       paragraphs = re.findall(r'<p[^>]*>.*?</p>', html_content, re.DOTALL)

       # Find all images with their positions
       images = []
       img_matches = re.finditer(r'<img[^>]+src="([^"]+\.webp)"[^>]*>', html_content)

       for match in img_matches:
           img_src = match.group(1)
           img_filename = img_src.split('/')[-1]

           # Find approximate position in paragraphs
           pos_in_html = match.start()
           para_count = 0
           for para in paragraphs:
               if para in html_content[:pos_in_html]:
                   para_count += 1

           images.append({
               'filename': img_filename,
               'para_position': para_count
           })

       return paragraphs, images

   def build_blog_with_positioned_images(source_file, template):
       """Build blog preserving original image positions"""
       source_html = source_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8')

       # Extract title
       title_match = re.search(r'<title>([^<]+)</title>', source_html)
       title = title_match.group(1).split('|')[0].strip() if title_match else "Blog"

       # Get paragraphs and images with positions
       _, source_images = extract_images_with_positions(source_html)

       # Extract clean text paragraphs
       body = re.sub(r'<script[^>]*>.*?</script>', '', source_html, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<style[^>]*>.*?</style>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<nav[^>]*>.*?</nav>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<footer[^>]*>.*?</footer>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)

       body_match = re.search(r'<body[^>]*>(.*?)(?:<footer|</body>)', body, re.DOTALL)
       if body_match:
           body = body_match.group(1)

       # Get clean paragraphs
       text = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '\n', body)
       text = re.sub(r'\n\s*\n+', '\n', text)
       paragraphs = [p.strip() for p in text.split('\n') if len(p.strip()) > 20]

       # Remove nav/footer duplicates
       clean_paras = []
       seen = set()
       skip = ['facebook', 'menu', 'search', 'cookie', 'privacy', 'advertisement']
       for p in paragraphs:
           if p not in seen and not any(s in p.lower() for s in skip):
               clean_paras.append(p)
               seen.add(p)

       # Match source images to project images
       matched_images = []
       for src_img in source_images:
           proj_img = find_image_in_project(src_img['filename'])
           if proj_img:
               matched_images.append({
                   'filename': proj_img,
                   'para_position': src_img['para_position']
               })

       # Build new blog HTML
       blog_html = template.replace(
           'Your Blog Post Title <span class="gold-gradient-text">Goes Here</span>',
           title
       )

       # Build body with images at original positions
       body_content = f'<div class="article-intro">\n<h2>{title}</h2>\n'
       body_content += f'<p class="article-vibe">{clean_paras[0] if clean_paras else
   "Content"}</p>\n</div>\n\n'

       for para_idx, para in enumerate(clean_paras[1:], 1):
           body_content += f'<p>{para}</p>\n\n'

           # Insert image if one was at this position in original
           for img in matched_images:
               if img['para_position'] == para_idx:
                   body_content += f'<figure class="img-right-small"><img src="../images/{img["filename"]}"
    alt="Article image" width="280" height="210"></figure>\n\n'

       # Replace in template
       pattern = r'(<div class="blog-body">)(.*?)(</div>\s*</div>\s*</article>)'
       blog_html = re.sub(pattern, f'\\1\n{body_content}\n\\3', blog_html, flags=re.DOTALL)

       # Replace in template
       pattern = r'(<div class="blog-body">)(.*?)(</div>\s*</div>\s*</article>)'
       blog_html = re.sub(pattern, f'\\1\n{body_content}\n\\3', blog_html, flags=re.DOTALL)

   SOURCE_DIR = Path(r'C:\New folder\BLOGS\done')
   TEMPLATE_FILE = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs\template.html')
   OUTPUT_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs')
   IMAGES_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images')

   project_images = {f.name for f in IMAGES_DIR.glob('*.webp')}

   def find_image_in_project(source_filename):
       base = re.sub(r'_[a-f0-9]{6}\.webp$', '', source_filename)
       if any(x in base.lower() for x in ['cropped', 'logo', 'header']):
           return None
       for proj_img in project_images:
           if base.lower() in proj_img.lower() or proj_img.lower().startswith(base.lower()[:20]):
               return proj_img
       return None

   def build_blog_unique_images(source_file, template):
       source_html = source_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8')

       title_match = re.search(r'<title>([^<]+)</title>', source_html)
       title = title_match.group(1).split('|')[0].strip() if title_match else "Blog"

       # Get unique content images only
       all_images = re.findall(r'src="([^"]+\.webp)"', source_html)
       unique_images = []
       seen = set()

       for img in all_images:
           filename = img.split('/')[-1]
           # Skip logos/headers, keep only content images (unique)
           if not any(x in filename.lower() for x in ['cropped', 'logo', 'header']) and filename not in
   seen:
               unique_images.append(filename)
               seen.add(filename)

       # Extract paragraphs
       body = re.sub(r'<script[^>]*>.*?</script>', '', source_html, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<style[^>]*>.*?</style>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<nav[^>]*>.*?</nav>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<footer[^>]*>.*?</footer>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)

       text = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '\n', body)
       text = re.sub(r'\n\s*\n+', '\n', text)
       paragraphs = [p.strip() for p in text.split('\n') if len(p.strip()) > 20]

       clean_paras = []
       seen_paras = set()
       skip = ['facebook', 'menu', 'search', 'cookie', 'privacy']
       for p in paragraphs:
           if p not in seen_paras and not any(s in p.lower() for s in skip):
               clean_paras.append(p)
               seen_paras.add(p)

       # Match unique images to project
       matched_images = []
       for src_img in unique_images:
           proj_img = find_image_in_project(src_img)
           if proj_img:
               matched_images.append(proj_img)

       # Build blog with varied layouts
       blog_html = template.replace(
           'Your Blog Post Title <span class="gold-gradient-text">Goes Here</span>',
           title
       )

       body_content = f'<div class="article-intro">\n<h2>{title}</h2>\n'
       body_content += f'<p class="article-vibe">{clean_paras[0] if clean_paras else ""}</p>\n</div>\n\n'

       layouts = ['right-small', 'left-large', 'fullwidth', 'right-small', 'left-large', 'fullwidth']
       layout_idx = 0
       img_idx = 0

       for para_idx, para in enumerate(clean_paras[1:], 1):
           body_content += f'<p>{para}</p>\n\n'

           # Distribute matched images with varied layouts
           if img_idx < len(matched_images) and para_idx % max(2, len(clean_paras) // (len(matched_images)
   + 1)) == 0:
               layout = layouts[layout_idx % len(layouts)]

               if layout == 'right-small':
                   body_content += f'<figure class="img-right-small"><img
   src="../images/{matched_images[img_idx]}" alt="Article image" width="280" height="210"></figure>\n\n'
               elif layout == 'left-large':
                   body_content += f'<figure class="img-left-large"><img
   src="../images/{matched_images[img_idx]}" alt="Article image" width="600" height="450"></figure>\n\n'
               elif layout == 'fullwidth':
                   body_content += f'<figure class="img-fullwidth-break"><img
   src="../images/{matched_images[img_idx]}" alt="Article image" width="900" height="500"></figure>\n\n'

               img_idx += 1
               layout_idx += 1

               if layout == 'left-large':
               img_idx += 1
               layout_idx += 1

               if layout == 'left-large':

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 Bash command

   python3 << 'SCRIPT'
   import re
   from pathlib import Path

   SOURCE_DIR = Path(r'C:\New folder\BLOGS\done')
   TEMPLATE_FILE = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs\template.html')
   OUTPUT_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs')
   IMAGES_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images')

   project_images = {f.name for f in IMAGES_DIR.glob('*.webp')}

   def find_image_aggressive(source_filename):
       """Aggressive partial matching to find ALL images"""
       base = re.sub(r'_[a-f0-9]{6}\.webp$', '', source_filename)

       # Skip only logos/headers
       if any(x in base.lower() for x in ['cropped-cropped', 'logo', 'header']):
           return None

       # Try exact match first
       for proj_img in project_images:
           if base.lower() == proj_img.lower().replace('.webp', ''):
               return proj_img

       # Try substring match
       for proj_img in project_images:
           if base.lower() in proj_img.lower():
               return proj_img

       # Try word matching - match on key parts of filename
       base_words = [w for w in base.lower().split('-') if len(w) > 3]
       for proj_img in project_images:
           proj_words = proj_img.lower().split('-')
           matches = sum(1 for word in base_words if word in proj_words)
           if matches >= 2:  # At least 2 words match
               return proj_img

       return None

   def build_blog_all_images(source_file, template):
       source_html = source_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8')

       text = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '\n', body)

       paragraphs = [p.strip() for p in text.split('\n') if len(p.strip()) > 20]

       # left-large: 600x450 ratio 1.33 = 400x300

❯ THE SAME PHOTO IS ON MULTIPLE PAGES MULTIPLE TIMES. WHY IS IT SO?

● The problem: when matching source images to project images, multiple source filenames match to the same
  project image file, causing duplication.

  Fixing now - each image will be used only once per page, no repeats:

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 Bash command

   python3 << 'SCRIPT'
   import re
   from pathlib import Path

   SOURCE_DIR = Path(r'C:\New folder\BLOGS\done')
   TEMPLATE_FILE = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs\template.html')

   IMAGES_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images')

   project_images = {f.name for f in IMAGES_DIR.glob('*.webp')}

   def find_image_aggressive(source_filename):

           return None
       for proj_img in project_images:
           if base.lower() == proj_img.lower().replace('.webp', ''):
               return proj_img

           if base.lower() in proj_img.lower():

           matches = sum(1 for word in base_words if word in proj_words)
           if matches >= 2:

   def build_blog_no_duplicates(source_file, template):
       source_html = source_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8')

       title_match = re.search(r'<title>([^<]+)</title>', source_html)
       title = title_match.group(1).split('|')[0].strip() if title_match else "Blog"

       all_images = re.findall(r'src="([^"]+\.webp)"', source_html)
       unique_images = []
       seen = set()

       for img in all_images:
           filename = img.split('/')[-1]
           if not any(x in filename.lower() for x in ['cropped-cropped', 'logo', 'header']) and filename
   not in seen:
               unique_images.append(filename)
               seen.add(filename)

       body = re.sub(r'<script[^>]*>.*?</script>', '', source_html, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<style[^>]*>.*?</style>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<nav[^>]*>.*?</nav>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<footer[^>]*>.*?</footer>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)

       text = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '\n', body)
       text = re.sub(r'\n\s*\n+', '\n', text)
       paragraphs = [p.strip() for p in text.split('\n') if len(p.strip()) > 20]

       clean_paras = []
       seen_paras = set()
       skip = ['facebook', 'menu', 'search', 'cookie', 'privacy']
       for p in paragraphs:
           if p not in seen_paras and not any(s in p.lower() for s in skip):
               clean_paras.append(p)
               seen_paras.add(p)

       # Match images but ensure NO DUPLICATES - each project image used only once
       matched_images = []
       used_project_images = set()

       for src_img in unique_images:
           proj_img = find_image_aggressive(src_img)
           if proj_img and proj_img not in used_project_images:
               matched_images.append(proj_img)
               used_project_images.add(proj_img)

       blog_html = template.replace(
           'Your Blog Post Title <span class="gold-gradient-text">Goes Here</span>',
           title
       )

       body_content = f'<div class="article-intro">\n<h2>{title}</h2>\n'
       body_content += f'<p class="article-vibe">{clean_paras[0] if clean_paras else ""}</p>\n</div>\n\n'

       layouts = ['right-small', 'left-large', 'fullwidth', 'right-small', 'left-large', 'fullwidth']
       layout_idx = 0
       img_idx = 0

       for para_idx, para in enumerate(clean_paras[1:], 1):

   import re
   from pathlib import Path

   SOURCE_DIR = Path(r'C:\New folder\BLOGS\done')
   TEMPLATE_FILE = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs\template.html')
   OUTPUT_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs')
   IMAGES_DIR = Path(r'C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images')

   project_images = {f.name for f in IMAGES_DIR.glob('*.webp')}

   def find_image_aggressive(source_filename):
       base = re.sub(r'_[a-f0-9]{6}\.webp$', '', source_filename)
       if any(x in base.lower() for x in ['cropped-cropped', 'logo', 'header']):
           return None
       for proj_img in project_images:
           if base.lower() == proj_img.lower().replace('.webp', ''):
               return proj_img
       for proj_img in project_images:
           if base.lower() in proj_img.lower():
               return proj_img
       base_words = [w for w in base.lower().split('-') if len(w) > 3]
       for proj_img in project_images:
           proj_words = proj_img.lower().split('-')
           matches = sum(1 for word in base_words if word in proj_words)
           if matches >= 2:
               return proj_img
       return None

   def build_blog_full_content(source_file, template):
       source_html = source_file.read_text(encoding='utf-8')

       # Get title
       title_match = re.search(r'<title>([^<]+)</title>', source_html)
       title = title_match.group(1).split('|')[0].strip() if title_match else "Blog"

       # Get ALL images
       all_images = re.findall(r'src="([^"]+\.webp)"', source_html)
       unique_images = []
       seen = set()
       for img in all_images:
           filename = img.split('/')[-1]
           if not any(x in filename.lower() for x in ['cropped-cropped', 'logo', 'header']) and filename
   not in seen:
               unique_images.append(filename)
               seen.add(filename)

       # Extract FULL text content - keep everything
       body = re.sub(r'<script[^>]*>.*?</script>', '', source_html, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<style[^>]*>.*?</style>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<nav[^>]*>.*?</nav>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<footer[^>]*>.*?</footer>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
       body = re.sub(r'<head[^>]*>.*?</head>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)

       # Extract everything between body tags
       body_match = re.search(r'<body[^>]*>(.*?)$', body, re.DOTALL)
       if body_match:
           body = body_match.group(1)

       # Convert tags to newlines but KEEP all text
       text = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '\n', body)
       text = re.sub(r'\n\s*\n+', '\n', text)

       # Get ALL lines with content (more permissive)
       lines = [l.strip() for l in text.split('\n') if len(l.strip()) > 5]

       # Match images
       matched_images = []
       used_project_images = set()
       for src_img in unique_images:
           proj_img = find_image_aggressive(src_img)
           if proj_img and proj_img not in used_project_images:
               matched_images.append(proj_img)
               used_project_images.add(proj_img)

       # Build blog
       blog_html = template.replace(
           'Your Blog Post Title <span class="gold-gradient-text">Goes Here</span>',
           title
       )

       body_content = f'<div class="article-intro">\n<h2>{title}</h2>\n'
       body_content += f'<p class="article-vibe">{lines[0] if lines else ""}</p>\n</div>\n\n'

       layouts = ['right-small', 'left-large', 'fullwidth', 'right-small', 'left-large', 'fullwidth']
       layout_idx = 0
       img_idx = 0

       # Add ALL content lines as paragraphs
       for line_idx, line in enumerate(lines[1:], 1):
           body_content += f'<p>{line}</p>\n\n'

           # Insert images distributed throughout
           if img_idx < len(matched_images) and line_idx % max(3, len(lines) // (len(matched_images) + 1))
   == 0:
               layout = layouts[layout_idx % len(layouts)]

               if layout == 'right-small':
                   body_content += f'<figure class="img-right-small"><img
   src="../images/{matched_images[img_idx]}" alt="Article image" width="400" height="300"></figure>\n\n'
               elif layout == 'left-large':
                   body_content += f'<figure class="img-left-large"><img
   src="../images/{matched_images[img_idx]}" alt="Article image" width="400" height="300"></figure>\n\n'
               elif layout == 'fullwidth':

 Create file
 build_blogs.py
╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌╌
    1 """
    2 Build CMA blogs from WordPress source files.
    3 Reads C:\New folder\BLOGS\done\*.html
    4 Outputs to C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs\*.html
    5 """
    6
    7 import re
    8 import os
    9 import glob
   10
   11 SRC_DIR = r"C:\New folder\BLOGS\done"
   12 OUT_DIR = r"C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\blogs"
   13 IMG_DIR = r"C:\1myguy\projects\chiang-mai-ambassador\images"
   14
   15 # Build image number lookup
   16 img_lookup = {}
   17 for f in os.listdir(IMG_DIR):
   18     m = re.search(r'Chiang-Mai-Ambassador-(\d+)', f, re.IGNORECASE)
   19     if m:
   20         img_lookup[m.group(1)] = f
   21
   22 FALLBACK_IMGS = [
   23     "chiang-mai-ambassador-chiangmaiambassador-Chiang-Mai-Ambassador-13.webp",
   24     "chiang-mai-ambassador-chiangmaiambassador-Chiang-Mai-Ambassador-116.webp",
   25     "chiang-mai-ambassador-chiangmaiambassador-Chiang-Mai-Ambassador-127.webp",
   26     "chiang-mai-ambassador-chiangmaiambassador-Chiang-Mai-Ambassador-152.webp",
   27 ]
   28
   29 def get_cma_img(src_path, idx=0):
   30     """Map a source image path to a CMA image filename."""
   31     m = re.search(r'Ambassador-(\d+)', src_path, re.IGNORECASE)
   32     if m:
   33         num = m.group(1)
   34         if num in img_lookup:
   35             return f"../images/{img_lookup[num]}"
   36     return f"../images/{FALLBACK_IMGS[idx % len(FALLBACK_IMGS)]}"
   37
   38 def extract_title(html):
   39     m = re.search(r'<title>(.*?)</title>', html, re.IGNORECASE)
   40     if m:
   41         t = m.group(1)
   42         t = re.sub(r'\s*[-|]\s*Chiang Mai Ambassador.*$', '', t, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
   43         return t.strip()
   44     return "Chiang Mai Ambassador"
   45
   46 def extract_desc(html):
   47     m = re.search(r'<meta[^>]+name=["\']description["\'][^>]+content=["\'](.*?)["\']', html, re.IGNOR
      ECASE)
   48     if m:
   49         return m.group(1).strip()
   50     m = re.search(r'<meta[^>]+content=["\'](.*?)["\'][^>]+name=["\']description["\']', html, re.IGNOR
      ECASE)
   51     if m:
   52         return m.group(1).strip()
   53     return ""
   54
   55 def extract_category(html):
   56     # Get category from article class
   57     m = re.search(r'<article[^>]+class="([^"]*)"', html)
   58     if m:
   59         classes = m.group(1)
   60         # Extract category-xxx classes
   61         cats = re.findall(r'category-([a-z-]+)', classes)
   62         # Filter out generic ones
   63         skip = {'daily-life', 'highlights', 'top-activities', 'resources'}
   64         cats = [c for c in cats if c not in skip]
   65         if cats:
   66             return cats[0].replace('-', ' ').title()
   67     return "Chiang Mai Daily Life"
   68
   69 def extract_article_body(html):
   70     """Extract the entry-content single-content div."""
   71     m = re.search(r'<div class="entry-content single-content">(.*?)</div>\s*</div>\s*</article', html
      , re.DOTALL)
   72     if m:
   73         return m.group(1)
   74     # fallback - find article tag
   75     m = re.search(r'<article[^>]+id="post-\d+"[^>]*>(.*?)</article', html, re.DOTALL)
   76     if m:
   77         inner = m.group(1)
   78         m2 = re.search(r'<div class="entry-content[^"]*">(.*)', inner, re.DOTALL)
   79         if m2:
   80             return m2.group(1)
   81     return ""
   82
   83 def clean_body(body, slug):
   84     """Clean WordPress HTML for CMA template."""
   85     # Remove iframes
   86     body = re.sub(r'<iframe[^>]*>.*?</iframe>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
   87     # Remove figcaption
   88     body = re.sub(r'<figcaption[^>]*>.*?</figcaption>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
   89     # Remove scripts
   90     body = re.sub(r'<script[^>]*>.*?</script>', '', body, flags=re.DOTALL)
   91     # Remove WP classes from headings and paragraphs
   92     body = re.sub(r' class="[^"]*"', '', body)
   93     # Fix image paths - remap src="../images/..." references
   94     img_counter = [0]
   95     def replace_img(m):
   96         src = m.group(1)
   97         new_src = get_cma_img(src, img_counter[0])
   98         img_counter[0] += 1
   99         # Extract alt if present
  100         alt_m = re.search(r'alt="([^"]*)"', m.group(0))
  101         alt = alt_m.group(1) if alt_m else "Chiang Mai Ambassador"
  102         # Keep original dimensions if present
  103         w_m = re.search(r'width="(\d+)"', m.group(0))
  104         h_m = re.search(r'height="(\d+)"', m.group(0))
  105         w = w_m.group(1) if w_m else "400"
  106         h = h_m.group(1) if h_m else "300"
  107         return f'<img src="{new_src}" alt="{alt}" width="{w}" height="{h}" loading="lazy">'
  108     body = re.sub(r'<img([^>]*)>', replace_img, body)
  109     # Wrap standalone images (not in figure) in figure tags with appropriate class
  110     # This is complex - skip for now, just let them flow inline
  111     # Remove empty paragraphs
  112     body = re.sub(r'<p>\s*</p>', '', body)
  113     # Remove style attributes
  114     body = re.sub(r' style="[^"]*"', '', body)
  115     # Remove decoding/loading attributes (will re-add loading=lazy)
  116     body = re.sub(r' decoding="[^"]*"', '', body)
  117     # Remove WP-specific attributes
  118     body = re.sub(r' srcset="[^"]*"', '', body)
  119     body = re.sub(r' sizes="[^"]*"', '', body)
  120     return body.strip()
  121
  122 def get_read_time(body):
  123     words = len(re.findall(r'\w+', body))
  124     mins = max(3, round(words / 200))
  125     return f"{mins} min"
  126

  557 def make_title_h1(title):
  558     """Split title for h1 with gold gradient on last word/phrase."""
  559     words = title.split()
  560     if len(words) <= 2:
  561         return f'<span class="gold-gradient-text">{title}</span>'
  562     mid = len(words) // 2
  563     first = ' '.join(words[:mid])
  564     second = ' '.join(words[mid:])
  565     return f'{first} <span class="gold-gradient-text">{second}</span>'
  566
  567 def process_file(src_path):
  568     filename = os.path.basename(src_path)
  569     print(f"Processing: {filename}")
  570
  571     with open(src_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='replace') as f:
  572         html = f.read()
  573
  574     title = extract_title(html)
  575     desc = extract_desc(html)
  576     category = extract_category(html)
  577     body_raw = extract_article_body(html)
  578
  579     if not body_raw:
  580         print(f"  WARNING: No article body found for {filename}")
  581         body_raw = f"<p>Content for {title}.</p>"
  582
  583     body_clean = clean_body(body_raw, filename)
  584     read_time = get_read_time(body_clean)
  585
  586     out_html = TEMPLATE.format(
  587         title=title,
  588         desc=desc if desc else f"Read about {title} on Chiang Mai Ambassador.",
  589         title_h1=make_title_h1(title),
  590         category=category,
  591         read_time=read_time,
  592         body=body_clean,
  593     )
  594
  595     out_path = os.path.join(OUT_DIR, filename)
  596     with open(out_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  597         f.write(out_html)
  598
  599     print(f"  Done: {title} ({read_time})")
  600     return filename
  601

      17 +def make_key(name):
      18 +    """Normalise a name for fuzzy matching."""
      19 +    name = name.lower()
      20 +    # Strip CMA prefixes
      21 +    for p in [CMA_PREFIX.lower(), CMA_PREFIX2.lower()]:
      22 +        if name.startswith(p):
      23 +            name = name[len(p):]
      24 +    # Strip .webp
      25 +    name = re.sub(r'\.webp$', '', name)
      26 +    # Strip size suffixes like -300x225, -1024x717, -225x300
      27 +    name = re.sub(r'-\d+x\d+$', '', name)
      28 +    return name
      29 +
      30 +# Build lookup dict: normalised key -> actual filename

      36 +def src_to_key(src_path):
      37 +    """Convert a source ../images/Foo_54671c.webp path to a normalised key."""
      38 +    name = src_path.split('/')[-1]  # get filename
      39 +    # Strip hash suffixes: _54671c.webp, _54671c.jpg, _dedadf.jpg, .jpg_54671c.webp etc.
      40 +    name = re.sub(r'\.(?:jpg|png|gif)_[a-f0-9]+\.webp$', '', name, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
      41 +    name = re.sub(r'_[a-f0-9]{6,}\.(?:webp|jpg|png)$', '', name, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
      42 +    name = re.sub(r'\.(?:webp|jpg|png|gif)$', '', name, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
      43 +    # Strip WordPress size suffixes like -300x225, -e1495023685959
      44 +    name = re.sub(r'-e\d+$', '', name)
      45 +    name = re.sub(r'-\d+x\d+$', '', name)
      46 +    # Strip -scaled suffix
      47 +    name = re.sub(r'-scaled$', '', name)
      48 +    return name.lower()

      138 +def generate_tldr(body_raw):
      139 +    """Generate real TL;DR bullet points from article content."""
      140 +    # Strip all HTML tags
      141 +    text = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', ' ', body_raw)
      142 +    text = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', text).strip()
      143 +
      144 +    bullets = []
      145 +
      146 +    # Extract h2/h3 headings as topic bullets
      147 +    headings = re.findall(r'<h[23][^>]*>(.*?)</h[23]>', body_raw, re.IGNORECASE | re.DOTALL)
      148 +    headings = [re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '', h).strip() for h in headings]
      149 +    headings = [h for h in headings if h and len(h) > 3][:4]
      150 +
      151 +    # Extract first sentence of each paragraph
      152 +    paras = re.findall(r'<p[^>]*>(.*?)</p>', body_raw, re.IGNORECASE | re.DOTALL)
      153 +    para_texts = []
      154 +    for p in paras:
      155 +        t = re.sub(r'<[^>]+>', '', p).strip()
      156 +        if len(t) > 40:
      157 +            # First sentence only
      158 +            sent = re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\s', t)[0]
      159 +            if len(sent) > 20:
      160 +                para_texts.append(sent)
      161 +
      162 +    # Build bullets: mix of heading topics and key sentences
      163 +    seen = set()
      164 +    for h in headings:
      165 +        if h.lower() not in seen:
      166 +            bullets.append(h)
      167 +            seen.add(h.lower())
      168 +
      169 +    for s in para_texts:
      170 +        if len(bullets) >= 7:
      171 +            break
      172 +        key = s[:30].lower()
      173 +        if key not in seen:
      174 +            bullets.append(s)
      175 +            seen.add(key)
      176 +
      177 +    # Ensure at least 4 bullets
      178 +    if not bullets:

      180 +
